  <script data-qa="Script.MetaViewport">
   function isTablet() {
            var tabletMinWidth  = 600;
            var desktopMaxWidth = 1136;
            return screen.width > tabletMinWidth
                && screen.width < desktopMaxWidth
                && navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad|Kindle|Tablet/i);
        }

        if (isTablet()) {
        	console.log('HACK: tablet detected - setting viewport ');
            var viewportElement = document.getElementById('MetaViewport');
            // iPad Pro in iOSApp 
            if (navigator.userAgent.match(/2048; 2732/)){
            	viewportElement.setAttribute('content', 'width=1380');
            }
            else {
              console.log('HACK: tablet detected - setting viewport ');
              viewportElement.setAttribute('content', 'width=990');
            }
            viewportElement.setAttribute('data-detect-viewport-is-scaled', 'true');
            
        }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function getQueryParameterByName(name) {
    var match = RegExp('[?&]' + name + '=([^&]*)').exec(window.location.search);
    return match && decodeURIComponent(match[1].replace(/\+/g, ' '));
}
function getCookie(cname) {
	var name = cname + "=";
	var decodedCookie = decodeURIComponent(document.cookie);
	var ca = decodedCookie.split(';');
	for(var i = 0; i <ca.length; i++) {
		var c = ca[i];
		while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') {
			c = c.substring(1);
		}
		if (c.indexOf(name) === 0) {
			return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
		}
	}
	return "";
}

         <script>
          function openTab(evt, tabName) {
  var i, tabcontent, tablinks;
  tabcontent = document.getElementsByClassName("toplistTabcontent");
  for (i = 0; i < tabcontent.length; i++) {
    tabcontent[i].style.display = "none";
  }
  tablinks = document.getElementsByClassName("toplistTablinks");
  for (i = 0; i < tablinks.length; i++) {
    tablinks[i].className = tablinks[i].className.replace(" active", "");
  }
  document.getElementById(tabName).style.display = "block";
  evt.currentTarget.className += " active";
}
         </script>

           Die Gewinner der Weltcup-Gesamtwertungen im alpinen Ski-Weltcup sind nicht immer auch die Preisgeldkönige der Saison. Bei den Hahnenkammrennen der Herren in Kitzbühel oder beim Damen-Slalom in Flachau beispielsweise gibt es weit mehr als das Mindestpreisgeld zu holen. Das waren die Top-Verdiener im Weltcup-Winter.

           <li>

             Vor 50 Jahren
            </strong>
            beschließt die Bundesregierung den Bau für das AKW Zwentendorf.
           </li>
           <li>
            US-Schauspielerin
            <strong>
             Reese Witherspoon
            </strong>
            wird 45 Jahre alt.
           </li>
          </div>
          <div class="zumButtonContainer">
           <a class="zumButton zumButton--weiss" href="/panorama/kalenderblatt/das-geschah-am-22-maerz;art209543,3370237" title="Das geschah am 22. März">
            mehr lesen
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
        </article>
       </div>
      </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     window.addEventListener("loginControllerLoaded", function(event) {
  // NEWSLETTER-WIDGET
  if(!userData) {
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__email').show();
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__button').show();
      console.log('Newsletterwidget - NOT logged in');
  } else {
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__email').remove();
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__button').addClass('newsletter__form__button--loggedin');
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__button').html('Newsletter abonnieren');
      jQuery('#newsletter__form__button').show();    
      console.log('Newsletterwidget - logged in');
  }
});

     <div class="container container__row container__row--nav container__row--column">
      <h2 class="happyEnd__headline">
       <i class="fas fa-laugh-beam happyEnd__material">
       </i>
       <br/>
       Happy End
      </h2>
      <div class="container__row">
       <article class="dreierTeaserVertikal container__row container__col--12 container__col--md12 container__col--lg12 meldungstyp--artikel">
        <figure class="dreierTeaserVertikal__figure fcmscss-scaler-teaser-zweier container__col--12 container__col--md6 container__col--lg6">

function tvProgrammChannel(channelId){
	var url="/nachrichten/tv/";
	var data=oonObj.storage.jsonGet("oonTvProgram"); data.channel=channelId; oonObj.storage.jsonSave("oonTvProgram", data);
	window.location.href=url;
}
    </script>

// Configure the adblock detector
fcmsJs.load('extlib_jquery').onLoad(function() {
    //var enabledEl = document.getElementById('adb-enabled');
    //var disabledEl = document.getElementById('adb-not-enabled');
    var showOverlay = false;

    function adBlockDetected() {
        //enabledEl.style.display = 'block';
        //disabledEl.style.display = 'none';
        window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'adblockerDetected'});

        if (showOverlay === true && !oonObj.getCookie("iab_overlay")) {
            if (window.innerWidth >= 990) {
                var iab_overlay = jQuery('<div id="iab_overlay"> </div>');
                iab_overlay.appendTo(document.body);
                jQuery(document).keyup(function(e) {
                    if (e.keyCode == 27) {
                        iab_overlay.hide();
                        jQuery(document).unbind("keyup");
                    }
                });
                var abd_images = [4,5,6,7];
                var randnr = Math.floor(Math.random()*abd_images.length);
                iab_overlay.append('<div align="center"><img src="https://static1.nachrichten.at/oonup/images/adblocker-800x533px-'+abd_images[randnr]+'.png"><a href="#" onclick="jQuery(\'#iab_overlay\').hide(); return false;"><span>x</span></a></div>');
                oonObj.setCookie("iab_overlay",true,7);
                //ga('send', 'event', 'Adblocker Overlay (IAB)', 'View', 'sujet'+abd_images[randnr], { nonInteraction: true });
                window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'adblockerOverlay'});
            }
        }
    }
    function adBlockNotDetected() {
        //disabledEl.style.display = 'block';
        //enabledEl.style.display = 'none';
        if (showOverlay === true && oonObj.getCookie("iab_overlay")) {
            window.dataLayer.push({'event': 'adblockerDeactivated'});
        }
    }

    if (typeof window.adblockDetector === 'undefined') {
        adBlockDetected();
    } else {
        window.adblockDetector.init(
            {
                debug: true,
                found: function(){
                    adBlockDetected();
                },
                notFound: function(){
                    adBlockNotDetected();
                }
            }
        );
    }
});
   </script>
  </div>
